    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Contacts] AS [c]
        WHERE LTRIM(RTRIM(LOWER([c].[PhoneNumber]))) = @__Trim_0 OR LTRIM(RTRIM(LOWER([c].[FirstName]))) = @__Trim_1) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
